href=\"http://my.sats.edu.za/\">MySats Online Platform</a></h2>\n<hr>\n<p>MySats is a website that is the central hub of learning at SATS. It is the system that makes online distance learning possible, so you can do all your studies electronically wherever you live. MySats provides you with essential information for studying at SATS.</p>\n<p>To read more about MySats click <a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/what-is-mysats/\" target=\"_blank\">here</a>.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-4\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_left\">\n\t\t\n\t\t<figure class=\"wpb_wrapper vc_figure\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"vc_single_image-wrapper   vc_box_border_grey\"><img class=\"vc_single_image-img \" src=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/Tabs_01-336x300.jpg\" width=\"336\" height=\"300\" alt=\"Tabs_01-336x300\" title=\"Tabs_01-336x300\"></div>\n\t\t</figure>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>Connectivity</h2>\n<hr>\n<p>You are able to communicate with other students and your course tutor on <a href=\"http://my.sats.edu.za/\" target=\"_blank\">MySats</a>. Since the feeling of isolation is one of the great challenges of distance learning, sharing your journey with other students is a great help. Students are allowed direct access to their tutors through MySats.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-4\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_left\">\n\t\t\n\t\t<figure class=\"wpb_wrapper vc_figure\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"vc_single_image-wrapper   vc_box_border_grey\"><img class=\"vc_single_image-img \" src=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/Tabs_02-336x300.jpg\" width=\"336\" height=\"300\" alt=\"Tabs_02-336x300\" title=\"Tabs_02-336x300\"></div>\n\t\t</figure>\n\t</div>\n\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>Paced Learning</h2>\n<hr>\n<p>By assigning due dates for all assignments and completion dates for all courses, <a href=\"http://my.sats.edu.za/\" target=\"_blank\">MySats</a> helps you to pace your studies in such a way that you are able to complete your qualification in good time by doing one course in each three-month term. The assignment dates are spread out to make your time-management easy – you just need to work steadily to complete your course.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel\" id=\"1403883701852-6-5\" data-vc-content=\".vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-heading\"><h4 class=\"vc_tta-panel-title\"><a href=\"#1403883701852-6-5\" data-vc-accordion=\"\" data-vc-container=\".vc_tta-container\"><span class=\"vc_tta-title-text\">Postgraduate School</span></a></h4></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_left\">\n\t\t\n\t\t<figure class=\"wpb_wrapper vc_figure\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"vc_single_image-wrapper   vc_box_border_grey\"><img class=\"vc_single_image-img \" src=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/06/photodune-675615-happy-university-girl-s-520x378.jpg\" width=\"520\" height=\"378\" alt=\"Happy University Girl\" title=\"Happy University Girl\"></div>\n\t\t</figure>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2><a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/postgraduate/\">Postgraduate School</a></h2>\n<hr>\n<p>The PGS site is the online platform where students doing advanced theological studies and our postgraduate faculty collaborate and discuss topics of mutual interest. The platform supports students doing postgraduate courses as well as those doing thesis work. Students upload their assignments, thesis chapters and any other documents relevant to their studies and they have the peace of mind that these valuable sources will be securely kept and will remain readily accessible. The platform also provides information of relevance to students and faculty, as well as access to a wide range of research material. Access to the website is easy – once you are a registered student you will be assigned your username and password you will then be able to login to the postgraduate site.</p>\n<p>Read more about the <a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/postgraduate/\">Postgraduate School</a></p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel\" id=\"1378875435675-3-0\" data-vc-content=\".vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-heading\"><h4 class=\"vc_tta-panel-title\"><a href=\"#1378875435675-3-0\" data-vc-accordion=\"\" data-vc-container=\".vc_tta-container\"><span class=\"vc_tta-title-text\">Courses</span></a></h4></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_left\">\n\t\t\n\t\t<figure class=\"wpb_wrapper vc_figure\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"vc_single_image-wrapper   vc_box_border_grey\"><img class=\"vc_single_image-img \" src=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/06/1-25-520x378.png\" width=\"520\" height=\"378\" alt=\"1 (25)\" title=\"1 (25)\"></div>\n\t\t</figure>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2><a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/course-details-undergraduate-school/\">Courses</a></h2>\n<hr>\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Students complete a selection of compulsory and elective courses in their various undergraduate programmes. We have provided course descriptions for all courses, except the counselling courses, in video format where the tutor personally sketches the important aspects of the courses. These descriptions will give the student an idea of the expectations of the tutors.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/course-details-undergraduate-school/\" target=\"_blank\">Click here to see the Undergraduate Course Details</a><br>\n<a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/course-details-postgraduate-school/\" target=\"_blank\">Click here to see the Postgraduate Course Details</a></p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel\" id=\"1405609584402-6-0\" data-vc-content=\".vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-heading\"><h4 class=\"vc_tta-panel-title\"><a href=\"#1405609584402-6-0\" data-vc-accordion=\"\" data-vc-container=\".vc_tta-container\"><span class=\"vc_tta-title-text\">Pay Online </span></a></h4></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_left\">\n\t\t\n\t\t<figure class=\"wpb_wrapper vc_figure\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"vc_single_image-wrapper   vc_box_border_grey\"><img class=\"vc_single_image-img \" src=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/pay-online-2.jpg\" width=\"520\" height=\"378\" alt=\"pay-online-2\" title=\"pay-online-2\"></div>\n\t\t</figure>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2><a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/course-payment/\">Pay Online</a></h2>\n<hr>\n<p>This is a direct access to our <a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/course-payment/\">online payment facility</a>. Please remember when you make a payment using the online payment facility you must put your name and the title of your course or book in the required field. This will help our accounts department to identify your payment.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel\" id=\"1407156713060-7-2\" data-vc-content=\".vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-heading\"><h4 class=\"vc_tta-panel-title\"><a href=\"#1407156713060-7-2\" data-vc-accordion=\"\" data-vc-container=\".vc_tta-container\"><span class=\"vc_tta-title-text\">Crossroads</span></a></h4></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-4\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p><img class=\" vc_box_border_grey attachment-full\" src=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2014/08/Crossroads-logo-ENG.jpg\" alt=\"Crossroads-logo-ENG\" width=\"920\" height=\"762\"></p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-8\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2><a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/undergraduate/crossroads\">Crossroads</a></h2>\n<hr>\n<p>Crossroads is a pre-tertiary programme and a resource tool to help local churches run an in-house discipleship and leadership training programme. Crossroads provides the church with the material it needs to set up and run a quality training programme.</p>\n<p>The material comprises: ready-to-use lessons, comprehensive notes, student hand-outs, marketing materials, administration tools and much more.</p>\n<p><em> The Programme is available in English and Afrikaans.</em></p>\n<p>Why would an international Christian higher education distance learning institution create a pre-tertiary (i.e. before university) bible study programme?&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/crossroads-a-one-or-two-year-foundational-discipleship-programme-with-options/\">Click here to find out.</a></p>\n<p>For more information visit the <a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/undergraduate/crossroads\">Crossroads</a> page</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel\" id=\"1408109966078-8-8\" class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2><a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/conspectus/\">Conspectus</a></h2>\n<hr>\n<p>Conspectus is a refereed evangelical theological e-journal published biannually by the South African Theological Seminary. This journal is a publication for scholarly articles in any of the major theological disciplines. Conspectus aims to combine sound scholarship with a practical and readable approach.</p>\n<p>Click here to see the <a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/conspectus/\">Conspectus</a> volumes.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel\" id=\"1378876827621-4-10\" data-vc-content=\".vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-heading\"><h4 class=\"vc_tta-panel-title\"><a href=\"#1378876827621-4-10\" data-vc-accordion=\"\" data-vc-container=\".vc_tta-container\"><span class=\"vc_tta-title-text\">Studying at SATS</span></a></h4></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_left\">\n\t\t\n\t\t<figure class=\"wpb_wrapper vc_figure\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"vc_single_image-wrapper   vc_box_border_grey\"><img class=\"vc_single_image-img \" src=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/06/1-5-520x378.png\" width=\"520\" height=\"378\" alt=\"1 (5)\" title=\"1 (5)\"></div>\n\t\t</figure>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2><a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/study-sats/\">Advantages of Studying at SATS</a></h2>\n<hr>\n<p>When you study with SATS you meet a team of educators and administrators who are creative, innovative, dedicated and passionate about the way they teach and deliver their courses. We are aware that it is crucial to balance business, careers, home and studies. With this in mind we believe we offer advantages to any person who would like to study via the distance learning method:</p>\n<ul>\n<li>We strive to understand your needs as a student.</li>\n<li>We constantly look at better methods of delivery.</li>\n<li>We are accredited by the Council on Higher Education and registered by the Department of Higher Education.</li>\n<li>Our qualifications are widely recognised.</li>\n<li>We involve you, our student, in the process of learning improvements.</li>\n<li>Our administrators are thoroughly trained, responsive and polite.</li>\n<li>We use technology to its full capacity to save you time.</li>\n<li>We are an internationally recognised institution</li>\n</ul>\n<dl>\n<dd><a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/study-sats/\">Read More</a></dd>\n</dl>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel\" id=\"1379454237863-5-9\" data-vc-content=\".vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-heading\"><h4 class=\"vc_tta-panel-title\"><a href=\"#1379454237863-5-9\" data-vc-accordion=\"\" data-vc-container=\".vc_tta-container\"><span class=\"vc_tta-title-text\">Timetable </span></a></h4></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_left\">\n\t\t\n\t\t<figure class=\"wpb_wrapper vc_figure\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"vc_single_image-wrapper   vc_box_border_grey\"><img class=\"vc_single_image-img \" src=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/06/photodune-3998542-happy-guy-s-520x378.jpg\" width=\"520\" height=\"378\" alt=\"Happy guy\" title=\"Happy guy\"></div>\n\t\t</figure>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2>Timetable</h2>\n<hr>\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\">The Seminary’s academic year runs from 1 February 2017 to 31 January 2018. The year is divided into four three-month terms.</p>\n<ul style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<li>Term 1 – 1 Feb to 30 Apr</li>\n<li>Term 2 – 1 May to 31 July</li>\n<li>Term 3 – 1 Aug to 31 Oct</li>\n<li>Term 4 – 1 Nov to 31 Jan</li>\n</ul>\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\">The majority of undergraduate courses in the Higher Certificate in Christian Life (HCCL)&nbsp;and the Bachelor of Theology (B.Th.) run over a three-month term. Such courses are&nbsp;offered twice each year, either in Term 1 and 3 or in Term 2 and 4.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\">You will find the courses in each qualification ordered by the terms in which&nbsp;they are offered. You should select at least one course from each timeslot – that&nbsp;is, one each from Term 1, 2, 3 and 4 for the academic year. Although you are only&nbsp;required to complete three courses each year, to finish your qualification in reasonable&nbsp;time you need to average four courses each year.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Year Courses</strong><br>\nYear Courses, namely Practical Ministry 1,2 and 3, and Greek 1a, 1b, 2a, and&nbsp;2b, are courses that do not run over a fixed, three-month term. Instead, you have&nbsp;365 days from the day you register to complete all the assessment tasks for the&nbsp;course. There are no prescribed due dates, but after 365 days your registration&nbsp;for this course will end automatically.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div></div></div></div><div In addition, we have nearly 200,000 books in our online library. You are welcome to browse the wide range of outstanding titles to assist you in your research, via our online catalogue. For postgraduate students who cannot access our physical holdings in person, the librarian, Tawanda, will assist you by sending you digital copies of your requested research extracts.<br>\n<a href=\"https://cloud.collectorz.com/satslibrary/books/\" target=\"_blank\">Search the Library Catalogue</a></p>\n<p>Contact the Librarian <a href=\"mailto:library@sats.edu.za\" target=\"_blank\">library@sats.edu.za</a>.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/conspectus/\">Click here</a> to access our Conspectus Journal which is a repository of Academic articles and papers.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div></div>\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel\" id=\"1488871648895-c13daeb6-096d\" data-vc-content=\".vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-heading\"><h4 class=\"vc_tta-panel-title\"><a href=\"#1488871648895-c13daeb6-096d\" data-vc-accordion=\"\" data-vc-container=\".vc_tta-container\"><span class=\"vc_tta-title-text\">Prospectus</span></a></h4></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"su-document su-responsive-media-yes\"><iframe src=\"//docs.google.com/viewer?embedded=true&amp;url=https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/SATS-Prospectus-2017.pdf\" width=\"600\" height=\"1250\" class=\"su-document\"></iframe></div>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p><strong>Message from the Principal: Why study theology at SATS?</strong></p>\n<p>In the past, and to a lesser extent, the recent past, some denominations have argued that as long as the pastor has a Bible and the Holy Spirit, that is enough to equip him/her to preach. After all, the disciples did not go to Bible College, did they? Happily, one hears much less of that kind of reasoning these days and it is because more and more people have come to realise that in an age where the congregation is more intellectually astute (and more critical), and where Christianity has become subjected to the attacks of secular ideologies much more intensively, it is non-negotiable that our leaders are able to understand and clearly defend the core doctrines of the faith from a biblical perspective. To do that they need to be properly equipped by specialists in this area, namely seminary faculty.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_row-fluid highlight-row\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-4\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_center\">\n\t\t\n\t\t<figure class=\"wpb_wrapper vc_figure\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/ICHE-Certificate-799x1024.jpg\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"vc_single_image-wrapper   vc_box_border_grey\"><img width=\"234\" height=\"300\" src=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/ICHE-Certificate-234x300.jpg\" class=\"vc_single_image-img attachment-medium\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/ICHE-Certificate-234x300.jpg 234w, https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/ICHE-Certificate-768x984.jpg 768w, https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/ICHE-Certificate-799x1024.jpg 799w, https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/ICHE-Certificate-59x75.jpg 59w, https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/ICHE-Certificate-700x897.jpg 700w, https://www.sats.edu.za/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/ICHE-Certificate.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 234px) 100vw, 234px\"></a><figcaption class=\"vc_figure-caption\">Click to view larger image</figcaption>\n\t\t</figure>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-4\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2 style=\"color: #fff !important;\">Certificate of Financial Operational Effectiveness and Accountability</h2>\n<hr>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">SATS was the first institution in the world to receive the Certificate of Financial Operational Effectiveness and Accountability awarded by the International Council on Higher Education (ICHE).</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">To achieve this, we were subjected to a panel visit by a team of financial experts, who carefully scrutinised our financial systems and reviewed all documented accounting, financial and budgeting policies and procedures, and compared them to international best practice.</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">Those enrolling or partnering with SATS, can therefore be assured of our financial integrity and exemplary practice.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-4\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h2 style=\"color: #fff !important;\">SATS subscribes to the following</h2>\n<hr>\n<p><a href=\"http://www.bible-researcher.com/chicago1.html\" target=\"_blank\">The Chicago Statement</a><br>\n<a href=\"https://www.lausanne.org/content/covenant/lausanne-covenant\" target=\"_blank\">Lausanne Covenant</a><br>\n<a href=\"http://www.icete-edu.org/beirut/\" target=\"_blank\">Beirut Benchmark</a></p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_row-fluid highlight-row\"><div class=\"highlight-button wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-9\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>Distance learning can be defined as learning which takes place remotely, and in our case, online.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-3\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div
